      * Date of Slaughter from processing date
      *================================================================
      * Get oldest and most recent production dates for the order's items
      * Rtv Prod Dt Rn f/Or/It RT - Item Transaction Detail  * 
      * Move input parameters to subroutine local variables.
     C                     Z-ADDWCAIC3    WL0009           Company Number
     C                     Z-ADDP1C4NB    WL0010           Order Number
     C                     Z-ADDWCHGCD    WL0011           Item Code
     C                     Z-ADDYL0020    WL0012           Date From
     C                     Z-ADDYL0021    WL0013           Date To
     C                     MOVEL'Y'       WL0014    P      Status Flag 4
     C                     EXSR SMRVGN
      * Move subroutine local variables to output parameters.
     C                     Z-ADDWL0012    YL0020           Date From
     C                     Z-ADDWL0013    YL0021           Date To
      * * format dates
      * CASE: LCL.Date From             USR is Entered
     C           YL0020    IFNE 0                          *IF
      * CLC Format Date Range  XF - Export Doc Defaults  * 
     C                     CALL 'PDP4XFR'              90  CLC Format Date
     C                     PARM *BLANK    W0RTN   7
     C                     PARM YL0020    WQ0004  70       Date From
     C                     PARM YL0021    WQ0005  70       Date To
     C           YL0024    PARM YL0024    WQ0006 40        Text USR 40
     C                     PARM WBC6SX    WQ0007  2        ED Slg_Proc Dat
      *
     C           *IN90     IFEQ '1'
      * Call to program ended in error
     C                     MOVEL'Y2U0032' W0RTN
     C                     MOVEL*BLANKS   W0CLPG 10
     C                     MOVEL'PDP4XFR' W0CLPG
      * Send message '*Error occured on CALL...'
     C                     MOVEL'Y2U0032' ZAMSID
     C                     MOVEL'Y2USRMSG'ZAMSGF
     C                     MOVELW0CLPG    ZAMSDA           Message data
     C                     EXSR ZASNMS
     C                     END
      * Error detected?
     C           W0RTN     IFNE *BLANK
     C                     SETON                     99    *
     C                     END
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: *OTHERWISE
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    YL0024           Text USR 40
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     MOVELYL0024    WN0083           ED Date of Slau
      * * AUS form 9115-2
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    WUV5CD           Date From Alpha
     C                     MOVELYL0020    WUV5CD           Date From Alpha
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    WUV6CD           Date To Alpha
     C                     MOVELYL0021    WUV6CD           Date To Alpha
      * * format dates
      * CASE: WRK.Date From Alpha       USR NE WRK.Date To Alpha
     C           WUV5CD    IFNE WUV6CD                     *IF
     C                     Z-ADD1         ZQ      50
     C           WUV5CD    CAT  'To':ZQ   WUXMTX    P      Text USR 12
     C                     Z-ADD1         ZQ      50
     C           WUXMTX    CAT  WUV6CD:ZQ WN0084    P      ED Slaughter Da
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: *OTHERWISE
      * * Don't format TO date if same as FROM date
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    WN0084           ED Slaughter Da
     C                     MOVELWUV5CD    WN0084           ED Slaughter Da
     C                     END                             *FI

      * * Get oldest and most recent production dates for the order's ite
      * Rtv Prod Dt Rn f/Or/It RT - Item Transaction Detail  * 
      * Move input parameters to subroutine local variables.

     C                     Z-ADDWCHGCD    WL0011           Item Code
     C                     Z-ADDYL0020    WL0012           Date From
     C                     Z-ADDYL0021    WL0013           Date To
     C                     MOVEL'N'       WL0014    P      Status Flag 4
     C                     EXSR SMRVGN
      * Move subroutine local variables to output parameters.
     C                     Z-ADDWL0012    YL0020           Date From
     C                     Z-ADDWL0013    YL0021           Date To
      * * format dates
      * CASE: LCL.Date From             USR is Entered
     C           YL0020    IFNE 0                          *IF
      * CLC Format Date Range  XF - Export Doc Defaults  * 
     C                     CALL 'PDP4XFR'              90  CLC Format Date
     C                     PARM *BLANK    W0RTN   7
     C                     PARM YL0020    WQ0008  70       Date From
     C                     PARM YL0021    WQ0009  70       Date To
     C           YL0024    PARM YL0024    WQ0010 40        Text USR 40
     C                     PARM WBC6SX    WQ0011  2        ED Slg_Proc Dat
      *
     C           *IN90     IFEQ '1'
      * Call to program ended in error
     C                     MOVEL'Y2U0032' W0RTN
     C                     MOVEL*BLANKS   W0CLPG 10
     C                     MOVEL'PDP4XFR' W0CLPG
      * Send message '*Error occured on CALL...'
     C                     MOVEL'Y2U0032' ZAMSID
     C                     MOVEL'Y2USRMSG'ZAMSGF
     C                     MOVELW0CLPG    ZAMSDA           Message data
     C                     EXSR ZASNMS
     C                     END
      * Error detected?
     C           W0RTN     IFNE *BLANK
     C                     SETON                     99    *
     C                     END
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: *OTHERWISE
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    YL0024           Text USR 40
     C                     END                             *FI
      * * RUS form 9450-3
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    WUV5CD           Date From Alpha
     C                     MOVELYL0020    WUV5CD           Date From Alpha
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    WUV6CD           Date To Alpha
     C                     MOVELYL0021    WUV6CD           Date To Alpha
      * *format dates
      * CASE: WRK.Date From Alpha       USR NE WRK.Date To Alpha
     C           WUV5CD    IFNE WUV6CD                     *IF
     C                     Z-ADD1         ZQ      50
     C           WUV5CD    CAT  'To':ZQ   WUXMTX    P      Text USR 12
     C                     MOVELYL0024    WN0085           ED Production D
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: *OTHERWISE
      * * Don't format TO date if same as FROM date
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    WN0085           ED Production D
     C                     MOVELWUV5CD    WN0085           ED Production D
     C                     END                             *FI

     CSR         UBEXIT    ENDSR
      /EJECT

     C           ZAPGMQ    IFEQ *BLANK
